						<strong class="fnt_c blk clr-pry" style="width: 170%;">Rules and Guidelines</strong>
						<em class="blk clr-txt full" style="width: 170%; text-align: left !important;">We have established the following rules:</em>
					<em class="blk clr-txt full" style="width: 170%; text-align: left !important;">- Dogs must be non-aggressive and well-socialized with other dogs.</em>
					<em class="blk clr-txt full" style="width: 170%; text-align: left !important;">- All dogs must be spayed / neutered if over six months of age.</em>
					<em class="blk clr-txt full" style="width: 170%; text-align: left !important;">- Dogs exhibiting signs of illness or injury will be separated and evaluated by our staff.</em>
					<em class="blk clr-txt full" style="width: 170%; text-align: left !important;">- Owners are expected to respect staff and to follow posted rules to maintain order and safety.</em>

            dimension4: getVedValue('subResultPosition'),
            dimension5: getVedValue('page')
            });
    }
    function getVedValue(key) {
        var ret = w.VedDecode[key];
        return ret ? ret + '' : '(not set)';
    }
})(window);
